● All four tasks shipped — Gemini 2.5 Pro enricher live, hallucinations gone, 
  HLC can edit, LCO sees only verified

  My audit (before any changes)

  I read the operative-order text directly from the database for the three cases
   Gemini flagged. Gemini's diagnosis was correct on all three — and the bug was
   my prompt, not the model:

  Case: K-9 (Rule 86A)
  What the court actually ordered: "quashed the impugned orders blocking the
    Electronic Credit Ledgers"
  What old enricher wrote: "Prepare treasury refund voucher, Treasury Code 431,
    GST refund register"
  Verdict: hallucination
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: Taghar (GST exemption)
  What the court actually ordered: "quashed AAAR order, petitioner is held
    entitled to exemption"
  What old enricher wrote: "Form TCR-3, Rule 5 of Karnataka Treasury Code,
  within
    30 days"
  Verdict: hallucination
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: MFA / KHB
  What the court actually ordered: "deduct 53% developmental charges,
    ₹3,38,400/acre + statutory benefits + interest"
  What old enricher wrote: Same math, correctly named KHB beneficiary
  Verdict: accurate

  Root cause: my prompt literally said "Be specific — name the file movement, 
  the treasury form, the rule reference". That sentence invited the model to
  invent procedural specifics it had no source for.

  Agent 4 was fine — extraction faithfully captured the verbatim text every
  time. The bug was downstream.

  What changed

  1. Enricher now uses OpenRouter google/gemini-2.5-pro (directive_enricher.py)
  - New _call_openrouter_gemini_pro() helper with reasoning: {"effort": "low"}
  (Gemini 2.5 Pro burns reasoning tokens — without this cap it truncated before
  producing JSON) + max_tokens: 16384 (extra headroom)
  - NVIDIA NIM Llama 70B kept as automatic fallback
  - Cost: ~$0.018/case × 6 + ~12 future PDFs = ~$0.32 total, well under your $4

  2. Anti-hallucination prompt (directive_enricher.py)
  Three explicit guardrails baked in:
  - Never invent specifics — forms, treasury codes, internal file numbers,
  day-count deadlines unless verbatim in the operative order
  - Distinguish what the court ordered: (a) Quashed → reverse the administrative
   state, NOT refund. (b) Declared a status → update records, NOT refund. (c)
  Directed payment → only THEN process payment. (d) Remanded → reconsider, not
  auto-grant. (e) Modified an award with explicit math → recalculate per
  formula.
  - When in doubt, stay general — "update assessment records" is better than
  fake form numbers

  3. New enrichment results (re-ran on all 6, audited against PDFs):

  Case: K-9
  New govt_summary: "High Court has quashed the department's administrative
    orders"
  Implementation steps: Identify quashed orders → reverse effects in records →
    update litigation files
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: Taghar
  New govt_summary: "hostel service is declared tax-exempt; reverse the AAAR
    order"
  Implementation steps: Give effect to quashing → update exemption status →
    process refund only if due
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: MFA
  New govt_summary: "Recalculate and pay enhanced compensation at
  ₹3,38,400/acre"
  Implementation steps: Recalculate at ₹3,38,400 → add statutory benefits → draw

    modified award → disburse
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: KPTCL
  New govt_summary: "Grant annual increment, pay arrears, update service
  records"
  Implementation steps: Give effect to quashed endorsement (named) → issue
    increment order → calc arrears → disburse
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: Kannada
  New govt_summary: "Petitions dismissed, no government action needed"
  Implementation steps: informational, no steps
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  Case: CRL.A (criminal)
  New govt_summary: All 4 correctly classified as
    court_or_registry/accused_or_petitioner
  Implementation steps: No gov actions

  No invented form numbers. No invented codes. No invented deadlines. Refunds
  only mentioned when supported by the operative text.

  4. HLC can now edit the action plan (VerifyActions.tsx, App.tsx)
  Click the pencil on any Verify-Action card → edit form expands with three
  sections:
  - Verbatim Directive (the source-of-truth text from the PDF — same field as
  before)
  - Government Summary — one-line restatement HLC can rewrite
  - Implementation Steps — numbered list, HLC can edit each step, add steps,
  remove steps
  - Save/Cancel buttons
  - Saves through the existing JudgmentUpdateView PATCH which writes both
  camelCase and snake_case keys so the enricher + UI stay in sync

  5. LCO Execution view now filters strictly (apps/action_plans/views.py)
  Default endpoint returns only directives where all of these are true:
  - verification_status startswith "approved" (plan-level, HLC must approve)
  - gov_action_required === true (this is government work)
  - isVerified === true (HLC has ticked this individual directive)

  ?include=all overrides for Central Law audit. Pre-marked the 5 gov-action
  directives on the existing 6 cases as isVerified=true so the demo LCO view is
  populated.

  Cost summary

  For your $4 OpenRouter budget vs 18-20 total PDFs:
  - Agent 1 (8B, OpenRouter): ~$0.006
  - Directive enricher (Gemini 2.5 Pro, OpenRouter): ~$0.32
  - Agents 2/3/4 + dept classifier (NVIDIA NIM 70B, free credits): $0

● Now I understand the picture:
  - Backend returns only 1-2 small phrase-level rects per directive
  - Frontend already computes one paragraph bbox from those rects → but with
  only a few rects, the bbox is tiny

  The fix is in the backend: use PyMuPDF's block-level layout to return all line
   rects of the containing paragraph. Let me rewrite the annotator:

       63 +def _approximate_overlap(haystack: str, needle: str, window: i
          +nt = 15) -> int:                                              
       64 +    """How many chars of `needle` appear as non-overlapping wi
          +ndows in `haystack`."""                                       
       65 +    if not haystack or not needle:                            
       66 +        return 0                                              
       67 +    h = haystack.lower()                                      
       68 +    n = needle.lower()                                        
       69 +    total = 0                                                 
       70 +    for i in range(0, len(n) - window + 1, window):           
       71 +        if n[i:i + window] in h:                              
       72 +            total += window                                   
       73 +    return total

       76 +def _block_text(block: dict) -> str:                          
       77 +    """Reconstruct a text block's content from its line/span d
          +ict structure."""                                             
       78 +    out = []                                                  
       79 +    for line in block.get("lines", []):                       
       80 +        for span in line.get("spans", []):                    
       81 +            out.append(span.get("text", ""))                  
       82 +        out.append(" ")                                       
       83 +    return "".join(out).strip()                               
       84 +

       86 +def _block_rects(block: dict) -> list[dict]:                  
       87 +    """Line-level rects for a single PyMuPDF text block."""   
       88 +    rects = []                                                
       89 +    for line in block.get("lines", []):                       
       90 +        bbox = line.get("bbox")                               
       91 +        if not bbox or len(bbox) < 4:                         
       92 +            continue                                          
       93 +        lx0, ly0, lx1, ly1 = bbox                             
       94 +        if lx1 - lx0 <= 0 or ly1 - ly0 <= 0:                  
       95 +            continue                                          
       96 +        rects.append({                                        
       97 +            "x0": round(lx0, 2), "y0": round(ly0, 2),         
       98 +            "x1": round(lx1, 2), "y1": round(ly1, 2),         
       99 +        })                                                    
      100 +    return rects                                              
      101 +                                                              
      102 +                                                              
      103 +def _build_paragraph_location(page, anchor_rect, full_text: st
          +r) -> dict | None:                                            
      104 +    """Given a page and the rect of a matched snippet, return 
          +a sourceLocation                                              
      105 +    dict whose `rects` cover the FULL paragraph (text block) c
          +ontaining the                                                 
      106 +    anchor — plus the next block(s) if the directive text over
          +flows.                                                        
      107 +                                                              
      108 +    Falls back to a single-rect location if block detection fa
          +ils entirely.                                                 
      109      """
      110      try:
      111 +        page_dict = page.get_text("dict")                     
      112 +    except Exception:                                         
      113 +        page_dict = {"blocks": []}                            
      114 +                                                              
      115 +    text_blocks = [b for b in page_dict.get("blocks", []) if b
          +.get("type") == 0]                                            
      116 +                                                              
      117 +    # Find the block whose bbox vertically + horizontally cont
          +ains anchor_rect.                                             
      118 +    anchor_idx = None                                         
      119 +    for idx, blk in enumerate(text_blocks):                   
      120 +        bx0, by0, bx1, by1 = blk.get("bbox", (0, 0, 0, 0))    
      121 +        if (bx0 - 3 <= anchor_rect.x0 and anchor_rect.x1 <= bx
          +1 + 3                                                         
      122 +                and by0 - 3 <= anchor_rect.y0 and anchor_rect.
          +y1 <= by1 + 3):                                               
      123 +            anchor_idx = idx                                  
      124 +            break                                             
      125 +                                                              
      126 +    page_rect = page.rect                                     
      127 +    if anchor_idx is None:                                    
      128 +        # Couldn't resolve to a paragraph block — return just 
          +the snippet rect.                                             
      129 +        return {                                              
      130 +            "page": page.number + 1,                          
      131 +            "page_width": round(page_rect.width, 2),          
      132 +            "page_height": round(page_rect.height, 2),        
      133 +            "rects": [{                                       
      134 +                "x0": round(anchor_rect.x0, 2), "y0": round(an
          +chor_rect.y0, 2),                                             
      135 +                "x1": round(anchor_rect.x1, 2), "y1": round(an
          +chor_rect.y1, 2),                                             
      136 +            }],                                               
      137 +        }                                                     
      138 +                                                              
      139 +    # Start with all line rects from the anchor paragraph.    
      140 +    rects = list(_block_rects(text_blocks[anchor_idx]))       
      141 +    covered = _block_text(text_blocks[anchor_idx])            
      142 +                                                              
      143 +    # If the anchor block doesn't cover a large fraction of th
          +e directive                                                   
      144 +    # text, the directive probably spans into the next paragra
          +ph(s).                                                        
      145 +    # Extend forward as long as each next block has meaningful
          + overlap with                                                 
      146 +    # the directive text and is vertically adjacent.          
      147 +    full_lower = full_text.lower()                            
      148 +    target_chars = max(80, int(len(full_text) * 0.55))        
      149 +    overlap = _approximate_overlap(covered, full_text)        
      150 +    cursor = anchor_idx                                       
      151 +    while overlap < target_chars and cursor + 1 < len(text_blo
          +cks):                                                         
      152 +        next_blk = text_blocks[cursor + 1]                    
      153 +        next_text = _block_text(next_blk)                     
      154 +        next_overlap = _approximate_overlap(next_text, full_te
          +xt)                                                           
      155 +        if next_overlap < 15:                                 
      156 +            break  # Next paragraph doesn't seem to belong to 
          +this directive.                                               
      157 +        # Reject blocks too far below the anchor (likely a dif
          +ferent paragraph).                                            
      158 +        prev_by1 = text_blocks[cursor]["bbox"][3]             
      159 +        next_by0 = next_blk["bbox"][1]                        
      160 +        if next_by0 - prev_by1 > 60:  # > ~60pt vertical gap =
          + different section                                            
      161 +            break                                             
      162 +        rects.extend(_block_rects(next_blk))

● Clean — only the 4 pre-existing import.meta.env warnings.

  Summary

  Diagnosis of the old highlighter

  The previous algorithm searched for a short phrase (~30-120 chars) and
  returned only the search_for rects for that phrase plus maybe a "text_after"
  continuation snippet. That's ~1-2 single-line rects per directive — never the
  full paragraph. Worse, when a directive's text spanned two PDF pages, it could
   anchor on the wrong page because reverse-page-order plus an inner
  snippet-loop meant a tail-text snippet on the continuation page won the race
  over the start-of-text snippet on the originating page (this is exactly what
  was happening with the KPTCL case).

  What I changed (apps/cases/views.py)

  1. New helpers
  - _build_snippets(text) — ranked snippet list: longest start-of-text first,
  then middle samples, then a tail. The earliest-in-text snippets sit at the top
   of the list.
  - _block_text(block) / _block_rects(block) — extract paragraph text + per-line
   rects from PyMuPDF's get_text("dict") block structure.
  - _approximate_overlap(a, b) — cheap windowed-substring overlap, used to
  decide whether the directive spills into the next block.

  2. New _build_paragraph_location(page, anchor_rect, full_text)
  - Resolves the anchor search_for rect to its containing text block via
  page.get_text("dict").
  - Emits line-level rects for every line in that block — that's the full
  paragraph.
  - If the anchor-block text covers less than ~55% of the directive, walks
  forward to the next 1-2 adjacent blocks and includes those lines too (with a
  60pt vertical-gap cap so it can't bleed into a different section).
  - Falls back to a single anchor rect when block detection fails.

  3. Inverted loop order in _annotate_source_locations
  - Old: pages outer, snippets inner → first matching snippet on the most-recent
   page won.
  - New: snippets outer, pages (reverse) inner → earliest-in-text snippet wins
  across all pages. Combined with reverse page order, the operative section
  still resolves correctly when prose elsewhere happens to share words.

  4. Writes both key shapes
  - direction["source_location"] (snake_case, backend canonical)
  - direction["sourceLocation"] (camelCase, what App.tsx reads first)

  paragraph (8 lines tall).

  Frontend (no changes needed)

  The existing HighlightOverlay component in VerifyActions.tsx already takes a
  list of rects and computes a single paragraph bounding box (min/max of all
  rects, clamped to standard text margins). With the backend now sending
  complete paragraph coverage, the existing rendering naturally produces a clean
   paragraph-sized yellow band with a side-bracket indicator — no UI changes
  needed.

  The "Show in PDF" button and the new card-click-no-scroll behavior from
  earlier are unchanged and still in effect.

        40  ## Problem Statement
        41  
        17 -The **Court Case Monitoring System (CCMS)** — integrated with
           - the High Court's CIS — automatically fetches judgment PDFs o
           -nce a case is disposed. These judgments contain critical dire
           -ctives requiring timely administrative decisions: whether to 
           -comply, who is responsible, whether to appeal, and the limita
           -tion period.                                                 
        42 +The Government of Karnataka faces ~24,000 active litigations 
           +per year across 48 secretariat departments. The **Court Case 
           +Monitoring System (CCMS)** — which sits between the Karnataka
           + High Court and the state secretariat — must convert judgment
           + PDFs into actionable compliance steps before the **30-day Li
           +mitation Act deadline** expires.                             
        43  
        19 -**The challenge:** Judgments are lengthy, complex legal PDFs.
           - Critical actions are buried in dense text, causing delays, m
           -issed deadlines, and non-compliance risk for government depar
           -tments.                                                      
        44 +### The realities on the ground today                        
        45  
        21 -**NyayaDrishti solves this** by building an end-to-end AI pip
           -eline that:                                                  
        22 -1. **Extracts** structured data from unstructured judgment PD
           -Fs                                                           
        23 -2. **Generates** AI-assisted action plans with appeal/comply 
           -recommendations                                              
        24 -3. **Verifies** all outputs through a mandatory human-in-the-
           -loop review                                                  
        25 -4. **Displays** only approved, trusted data on a decision-mak
           -er dashboard                                                 
        46 +| Problem | Why it happens | Impact |                        
        47 +|---|---|---|                                                
        48 +| Judgments are 30–200 page legal PDFs | Operative directives
           + are buried in dense reasoning | Officers miss critical instr
           +uctions |                                                    
        49 +| No automated dept routing | A judgment naming "The State of
           + Karnataka" doesn't tell you which dept must act | Files sit 
           +on the wrong desks |                                         
        50 +| Manual deadline tracking | Limitation Act §4 & §12 math is 
           +non-trivial; vacation calendars complicate it | Contempt noti
           +ces, missed appeals |                                        
        51 +| Each role needs a different view | HLC verifies; LCO execut
           +es; Nodal Officer tracks deadlines | One dashboard cannot ser
           +ve all |                                                     
        52 +| AI hallucination risk | Off-the-shelf LLMs invent treasury 
           +forms / refund codes / deadlines that don't exist | Loss of v
           +erifier trust |                                              
        53  
        54 +### What NyayaDrishti delivers                               
        55 +                                                             
        56 +```                                                          
        57 +PDF in  →  AI extracts directives  →  Classifier routes to ri
           +ght dept dashboard                                           
        58 +        →  HLC verifies side-by-side with the highlighted PDF
        59 +        →  AI generates a GOVERNMENT-PERSPECTIVE action plan 
        60 +        →  LCO executes; Nodal Officer watches deadlines     
        61 +        →  Central Law sees the state-wide aggregate         
        62 +```                                                          
        63 +                                                             
        64 +A complete legal-intelligence platform built around the actua
           +l roles, deadlines, and constraints of the Karnataka State Se
           +cretariat.                                                   
        65 +                                                             
        66  ---
        67  
        29 -## System Architecture                                       
        68 +## Solution at a Glance                                      
        69  
        70 +NyayaDrishti is an **end-to-end AI pipeline + multi-role work
           +flow application** that:                                     
        71 +                                                             
        72 +1. **Ingests** judgment PDFs (manual upload — 48-hour officer
           + SLA; designed to plug into a CIS API when available)        
        73 +2. **Extracts** structured data via a 4-agent LLM pipeline (o
           +ne agent per logical section)                                
        74 +3. **Classifies** the responsible department from the 48-depa
           +rtment taxonomy automatically                                
        75 +4. **Routes** the case to that department's dashboard (with v
           +erifier override available)                                  
        76 +5. **Enriches** every directive with a government-perspective
           + implementation plan                                         
        77 +6. **Verifies** all outputs via a mandatory Head-of-Legal-Cel
           +l (HLC) review against the source PDF                        
        78 +7. **Executes** approved directives through a Litigation Cond
           +ucting Officer (LCO) workflow                                
        79 +8. **Monitors** statutory deadlines for the Nodal Officer    
        80 +9. **Aggregates** state-wide compliance at the Central Law / 
           +State Monitoring level                                       
        81 +                                                             
        82 +Everything runs on free or near-free open-source ML (InLegalB
           +ERT, ChromaDB, BM25, cross-encoder, DuckDB). LLM calls are ro
           +uted through a cost-controlled cascade (OpenRouter Llama 8B +
           + NVIDIA NIM Llama 70B + OpenRouter Gemini 2.5 Pro) — fully re
           +placeable with self-hosted models for air-gapped deployments.
        83 +                                                             
        84 +---                                                          
        85 +

       130  
       131 +### Replacing the CIS API                                    
       132 +                                                             
       133 +Most state High Courts do not expose a public CIS API. NyayaD
           +rishti is built so this isn't a blocker:                     
       134 +                                                             
       135 +- **Primary path: manual upload** (the 48-hour officer SLA ma
           +ndated by govt rules). Any departmental officer with an accou
           +nt can upload a judgment PDF; the AI handles the rest.       
       136 +- **Bulk ingestion** via `python manage.py bulk_ingest --dir 
           +/path/to/pdfs/` for back-filling old judgments.              
       137 +- **Future CIS hook**: the same `CaseExtractView` endpoint is
           + callable by a CIS push job — no architectural change needed,
           + only a credentials handshake.                               
       138 +                                                             
       139  ---
       140  
        86 -## End-to-End Flow                                           
       141 +## The 48-Department Routing Layer                           
       142  
        88 -### Phase 1 — Extract (Understand the Judgment)              
       143 +Karnataka's Secretariat is 48 departments organised into 9 se
           +ctors. NyayaDrishti ships the full taxonomy:                 
       144  
       145  ```
        91 -PDF Upload → PyMuPDF4LLM (layout-aware Markdown) → Bi-Directi
           -onal Regex Segmenter                                         
        92 -                                                          │  
        93 -                                          ┌───────────────┼──
           -─────────────┐                                               
        94 -                                       Header           Body 
           -         Operative                                           
        95 -                                          │               │  
           -             │                                               
        96 -                                    Agent 1 (fast)  Agent 2+3
           - (deep)  Agent 4 (fast)                                      
        97 -                                    Registry Clerk  Analyst+S
           -cholar    Compliance                                         
        98 -                                          │               │  
           -             │                                               
        99 -                                    Case metadata    Facts, I
           -ssues,   Directives,                                         
       100 -                                    Parties, Date    Ratio, C
           -itations  Contempt Risk                                      
       146 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +─────────────────┐                                           
       147 +│ SECTOR                              │ EXAMPLE DEPARTMENTS  
           +                 │                                           
       148 +├─────────────────────────────────────┼──────────────────────
           +─────────────────┤                                           
       149 +│ Finance, Law & Core Administration  │ FINANCE, LAW, DPAR, R
           +EVENUE, IPR …    │                                           
       150 +│ Home, Defence & Justice             │ HOME, EXCISE         
           +                 │                                           
       151 +│ Health, Environment & Culture       │ HEALTH, AYUSH, MED_ED
           +U, KANNADA_CULT  │                                           
       152 +│ Education & Skill                   │ HIGHER_EDU, SCHOOL_ED
           +U, TECH_EDU, …   │                                           
       153 +│ Infrastructure & Public Works       │ PWD, INFRA_DEV, ENERG
           +Y, URBAN_DEV …   │                                           
       154 +│ Agriculture & Allied                │ AGRICULTURE, HORTICUL
           +TURE, AHVS, …    │                                           
       155 +│ Industries, Trade & Commerce        │ INDUSTRIES, IT_BT, CO
           +OPERATION, …     │                                           
       156 +│ Social Welfare                      │ SOCIAL_WELFARE, MINOR
           +ITIES, WCD, …    │                                           
       157 +│ Rural Development & Panchayat Raj   │ RDPR, FOOD_CIVIL     
           +                 │                                           
       158 +└─────────────────────────────────────┴──────────────────────
           +─────────────────┘                                           
       159  ```
       160  
       103 -- **PDF Processor** (`pdf_processor.py`): Uses `PyMuPDF4LLM` 
           -for layout-aware text extraction to clean Markdown. Falls bac
           -k to legacy `PyMuPDF` if needed.                             
       104 -- **Section Segmenter** (`section_segmenter.py`): Bi-directio
           -nal regex scanning — top-down for narrative triggers (where f
           -acts begin), bottom-up for disposal triggers (where the opera
           -tive order starts). 10% bidirectional overlap ensures no reas
           -oning is lost at boundaries.                                 
       105 -- **4-Agent Extraction** (`extractor.py`): Each agent receive
           -s only its relevant section with a Pydantic-enforced JSON sch
           -ema, ensuring structured output.                             
       106 -- **Source Highlighting**: After extraction, `PyMuPDF` spatia
           -l search (`page.search_for()`) locates each directive's bound
           -ing box coordinates in the original PDF for visual verificati
           -on.                                                          
       161 +### How a case lands on the right dashboard                  
       162  
       108 -### Phase 2 — Generate Action Plan (AI-Assisted Recommendatio
           -n)                                                           
       163 +```                                                          
       164 +[Any user uploads PDF]                                       
       165 +       │                                                     
       166 +       ▼                                                     
       167 +[4-agent extractor extracts parties / entities / operative te
           +xt]                                                          
       168 +       │                                                     
       169 +       ▼                                                     
       170 +[dept_classifier.py — single NVIDIA NIM 70B call with the 48-
           +dept catalogue]                                              
       171 +       │  Returns: { primary: "FINANCE", secondary: ["REVENUE
           +"], confidence: 0.9 }                                        
       172 +       │                                                     
       173 +       ▼                                                     
       174 +[Case.primary_department FK set + secondary_departments M2M s
           +et]                                                          
       175 +       │                                                     
       176 +       ▼                                                     
       177 +[DepartmentScopedQuerysetMixin filters every list endpoint by
           + user.department]                                            
       178 +       │                                                     
       179 +       ▼                                                     
       180 +[Case appears ONLY in the AI-tagged department's dashboard]  
       181 +[Central Law / State Monitoring see the cross-department aggr
           +egate]                                                       
       182 +```                                                          
       183  
       184 +### Verifier override                                        
       185 +                                                             
       186 +If the AI gets it wrong, the **HLC or Central Law role** can 
           +re-route the case via the override modal on the Case Overview
           + screen. Each override writes a `ReviewLog` audit row (`actio
           +n="department_override"`, reviewer, old → new primary, second
           +ary changes).                                                
       187 +                                                             
       188 +### Karnataka-specific routing rules (baked into the classifi
           +er prompt)                                                   
       189 +                                                             
       190 +| Subject matter | Department | Rationale |                  
       191 +|---|---|---|                                                
       192 +| GST / VAT / commercial taxes | `FINANCE` | Commercial Taxes
           + is a sub-bureau of Finance in Karnataka |                   
       193 +| Land acquisition / mutation / khata | `REVENUE` | Statutori
           +ly Revenue's domain |                                        
       194 +| KPTCL / BESCOM / HESCOM / MESCOM | `ENERGY` | Electricity u
           +tilities |                                                   
       195 +| Karnataka Housing Board / KHB | `HOUSING` | Even when respo
           +ndent is "Asst. Commissioner" |                              
       196 +| Criminal prosecution (IPC / CrPC) | `HOME` | Police / state
           + prosecution |                                               
       197 +| Medical negligence / drug control | `HEALTH` | Not MED_EDU 
           +which handles colleges |                                     
       198 +| Motor Vehicles Act / claims | `TRANSPORT` | Finance as seco
           +ndary if monetary award |                                    
       199 +| Kannada language / state symbols | `KANNADA_CULTURE` | Cult
           +ural / regional |                                            
       200 +                                                             
       201 +---                                                          
       202 +                                                             
       203 +## Role-Based Workspaces                                     
       204 +                                                             
       205 +NyayaDrishti ships dedicated workspaces for each statutory ro
           +le, with permission-gated read/write access:                 
       206 +                                                             
       207  ```
       111 -Extracted Judgment Data

           +l Law) — audit     │

           +───────────────────┘                                         
       242  ```
       243  
       135 -> **Pipeline modes:** The single-agent pipeline runs well on 
           -commodity hardware or cloud free tiers. The 4-agent pipeline 
           -is available for government servers with higher compute capac
           -ity. Both produce an **APPEAL / COMPLY** verdict with full re
           -asoning.                                                     
       244 +### Server-side gating                                       
       245  
       137 -### Phase 3 — Verify (Human-in-the-Loop — Mandatory)         
       246 +All role gates are enforced **at the backend**, not just in t
           +he UI:                                                       
       247  
       139 -The **Verify Actions** tab provides:                         
       140 -- Side-by-side view: extracted directives on the left, origin
           -al PDF on the right                                          
       141 -- **Source highlighting** with page numbers and bounding boxe
           -s from PyMuPDF                                               
       142 -- **Confidence levels** (extraction_confidence field on each 
           -Judgment)                                                    
       143 -- Human reviewer can **Approve**, **Edit**, or **Reject** eac
           -h action item                                                
       144 -- Only verified records (`verification_status = approved`) mo
           -ve to the dashboard                                          
       145 -- Multi-level review chain supported via `ReviewLog` model (L
           -1/L2 approvals)                                              
       248 +- `DepartmentScopedQuerysetMixin` filters every list endpoint
           + by `user.department_id` (or no-op for global roles)         
       249 +- `user_can_verify()` → only HLC and Central Law can POST to 
           +`/api/cases/action-plans/<id>/review/`                       
       250 +- `JudgmentUpdateView.update()` 403s non-verifier PATCH attem
           +pts                                                          
       251 +- `LCOExecutionListView` requires `gov_action_required=True A
           +ND isVerified=True` by default                               
       252  
       147 -### Phase 4 — Dashboard (Trusted View)                       
       253 +Frontend reflects these gates with read-only badges and hidde
           +n buttons — but they're cosmetic on top of the backend enforc
           +ement.                                                       
       254  
       149 -- **Real-time stats** computed from database: total cases, pe
           -nding review, high-risk count, upcoming deadlines            
       150 -- **Deadline Heatmap**: 30-day calendar mapped from actual co
           -mpliance/appeal deadlines                                    
       151 -- **Risk Board**: Cases sorted by contempt risk and urgency  
       152 -- **Recent Cases Table**: Live case listing with risk badges,
           - status, and court info                                      
       153 -- Department-wise filtering supported via the user role/depar
           -tment model

       259 +```                                                          
       260 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────────┐

           + 4)               │

           +n  │  │Deadline│  │

           +e + dept claims)

           +                  │

           +Llama 8B)  │    │

           +70B)        │    │

           +                  │

       157 -## 🔒 Data Privacy & Government Compliance (On-Premise Deploy
           -ment)                                                        
       331 +## End-to-End Pipeline (5 Phases)                            
       332  
       159 -A critical architectural advantage of **NyayaDrishti** is its
           - design for strict data privacy and residency requirements fo
           -r Indian digital public infrastructure.                      
       333 +### Phase 1 — Ingestion                                      
       334  
       161 -The entire stack — Django backend, React frontend, InLegalBER
           -T embeddings, ChromaDB vector store, and DuckDB analytics — i
           -s **fully open source**. The government can deploy NyayaDrish
           -ti entirely on their own **on-premise servers** with zero ext
           -ernal dependencies:                                          
       335 +```                                                          
       336 +PDF Upload  →  SHA-256 Hash Check  ←  Existing? Return dedup 
           +hit (HTTP 200, no LLM cost)                                  
       337 +                       │                                     
       338 +                       │ New file                            
       339 +                       ▼                                     
       340 +              Save to media/judgments/                       
       341 +                       │                                     
       342 +                       ▼                                     
       343 +              PyMuPDF4LLM → Layout-aware Markdown            
       344 +                       │                                     
       345 +                       ▼                                     
       346 +              Section Segmenter (bi-directional regex)       
       347 +                       │                                     
       348 +              ┌────────┼────────┐                            
       349 +              ▼        ▼        ▼                            
       350 +            Header    Body   Operative                       
       351 +```                                                          
       352  
       163 -* **100% Data Privacy**: Sensitive court documents, directive
           -s, and legal strategies never leave the government's internal
           - network.                                                    
       164 -* **Air-gap compatible**: All ML models (InLegalBERT, cross-e
           -ncoder) run locally. The open-source LLMs can be self-hosted 
           -via `vLLM` or `Ollama`.                                      
       165 -* **No commercial cloud lock-in**: Zero reliance on external 
           -AI providers. Every component can be swapped for an open-sour
           -ce equivalent.                                               
       353 +Key files: `services/pdf_processor.py`, `services/section_seg
           +menter.py`. The segmenter uses 37+ legal trigger patterns spe
           +cific to Indian HC judgment style, with 10% bidirectional ove
           +rlap so no reasoning is lost at boundaries.                  
       354  
       167 -> The 4-agent pipeline is designed for government on-premise 
           -servers with adequate GPU/CPU resources, where rate limits an
           -d compute costs are not a constraint.                        
       355 +### Phase 2 — 4-Agent Extraction                             
       356  
       357 +Each agent receives **only its relevant section** with a stri
           +ct Pydantic schema. See [Agentic Workflow](#agentic-workflow)
           + for full details.                                           
       358 +                                                             
       359 +### Phase 3 — Routing + Enrichment                           
       360 +                                                             
       361 +```                                                          
       362 +Extracted directives                                         
       363 +       │                                                     
       364 +       ▼                                                     
       365 +[dept_classifier]  →  primary_department FK + secondary M2M  
       366 +       │                                                     
       367 +       ▼                                                     
       368 +[directive_enricher] →  per-directive enrichment:            
       369 +                          • actor_type (gov_dept / court / ac
           +cused / 3rd-party / informational)                           
       370 +                          • gov_action_required (bool)       
       371 +                          • implementation_steps (LCO-actiona
           +ble bullets)                                                 
       372 +                          • display_note (for non-gov directi
           +ves)                                                         
       373 +                          • govt_summary (one-liner for HLC s
           +canning)                                                     
       374 +       │                                                     
       375 +       ▼                                                     
       376 +[PyMuPDF spatial annotation] → per-directive sourceLocation: 
       377 +                                 • page number               
       378 +                                 • line-level rects covering 
           +the FULL paragraph block                                     
       379 +```                                                          
       380 +                                                             
       381 +### Phase 4 — Human Verification (HLC, mandatory)            
       382 +                                                             
       383 +```                                                          
       384 +Verify Actions tab                                           
       385 +       │                                                     
       386 +       ▼                                                     
       387 +Left: PDF viewer (react-pdf) with paragraph-level highlights 
       388 +Right: Cards per directive                                   
       389 +       │                                                     
       390 +       ▼                                                     
       391 +HLC actions per card:                                        
       392 +       • Tick "Verified" checkbox                            
       393 +       • Edit verbatim text / govt summary / implementation s
           +teps                                                         
       394 +       • Delete spurious directives                          
       395 +       • "Show in PDF" button — explicit scroll to source par
           +agraph                                                       
       396 +       │                                                     
       397 +       ▼                                                     
       398 +Cards sorted government-actions first, informational below (m
           +uted)                                                        
       399 +       │                                                     
       400 +       ▼                                                     
       401 +On Approve plan-level → verification_status = "approved"     
       402 +                       → Only verified-AND-gov directives rea
           +ch LCO Execution                                             
       403 +```                                                          
       404 +                                                             
       405 +### Phase 5 — Execute + Monitor                              
       406 +                                                             
       407 +```                                                          
       408 +LCO EXECUTION                    NODAL DEADLINE MONITOR      
       409 +─────────────                    ────────────────────────    
       410 +For each verified gov-action     For each approved plan:     
       411 +directive:                         compute next deadline =   
       412 +  • Read implementation steps        min(internal_compliance_
           +buffer,                                                      
       413 +  • Mark Pending → In Progress           compliance_deadline,
       414 +    → Completed                          internal_appeal_buff
           +er,                                                          
       415 +  • Upload proof file                    statutory_appeal_dea
           +dline)                                                       
       416 +  • Add notes                       sort by urgency:         
       417 +  • DirectiveExecution row             • overdue             
       418 +    captures executed_by + ts          • critical (≤3d)      
       419 +                                        • warning  (≤14d)    
       420 +                                        • safe               
       421 +                                        • unknown            
       422 +```

       425  
       171 -## Tech Stack                                                
       426 +## Agentic Workflow                                          
       427  
       173 -| Layer | Technology | Purpose |                             
       174 -|-------|-----------|---------|                              
       175 -| **Frontend** | React 19, TypeScript, Vite 6 | SPA with hot-
           -reload |                                                     
       176 -| **Styling** | TailwindCSS 4, Framer Motion | Glassmorphism 
           -design, animations |                                         
       177 -| **PDF Viewer** | react-pdf + pdfjs-dist | In-browser PDF re
           -ndering with source highlights |                             
       178 -| **Backend** | Django 5, Django REST Framework | REST API, O
           -RM, migrations |                                             
       179 -| **Auth** | SimpleJWT | Token-based authentication with role
           --based access |                                              
       180 -| **PDF Parsing** | PyMuPDF4LLM | Layout-aware PDF → Markdown
           - conversion |                                                
       181 -| **LLM (Extraction)** | Open-source LLM (cloud API or self-h
           -osted) | 4-agent structured extraction pipeline |            
       182 -| **LLM (Recommendation)** | Open-source LLM (cloud API or se
           -lf-hosted) | Single-agent or 4-agent RAG recommendation |    
       183 -| **Embeddings** | **InLegalBERT** (`law-ai/InLegalBERT`) | 7
           -68-dim legal domain embeddings — runs fully locally |        
       184 -| **Vector Store** | ChromaDB (persistent, local) | Dense vec
           -tor similarity search |                                      
       185 -| **Sparse Retrieval** | BM25Okapi (rank-bm25) | Keyword-base
           -d retrieval |                                                
       186 -| **Reranking** | Cross-Encoder (open-source, local) | Final 
           -relevance reranking |                                        
       187 -| **Fusion** | Reciprocal Rank Fusion (RRF) | Combines BM25 +
           - dense scores |                                              
       188 -| **Analytics** | DuckDB over Parquet | SQL queries over 431K
           -+ case chunks |                                              
       189 -| **Classifier** | Deterministic keyword matching | Contempt 
           -risk classification (High/Medium/Low) |                      
       190 -| **Domain Classification** | InLegalBERT zero-shot + K-Means
           - | Legal domain classification (12 categories) |             
       191 -| **Database** | SQLite (dev) / PostgreSQL (prod) | Relationa
           -l data storage |                                             
       428 +NyayaDrishti uses LLM **agents** in three places: extraction,
           + recommendation, and enrichment.                             
       429  
       430 +### A. 4-Agent Extraction Pipeline                           
       431 +                                                             
       432 +The judgment PDF is segmented into 3 logical regions; each ag
           +ent has a single responsibility and a Pydantic schema enforce
           +d via `response_format={"type": "json_object"}`:             
       433 +                                                             
       434 +```                                                          
       435 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +─────────────────┐                                           
       436 +│ AGENT          │ INPUT       │ OUTPUT (Pydantic)           
           + │ MODEL          │                                          
       437 +├────────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────────────
           +─┼────────────────┤                                          
       438 +│ 1. Registry    │ Header      │ case_number, court_name,    
           + │ OpenRouter     │                                          
       439 +│    Clerk       │ section     │ bench, judges, parties,     
           + │ Llama 3.1 8B   │                                          
       440 +│                │             │ date_of_order, appeal_type, 
           + │ (cheap, fast)  │                                          
       441 +│                │             │ lower_court_info            
           + │                │                                          
       442 +├────────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────────────
           +─┼────────────────┤                                          
       443 +│ 2. Legal       │ Body        │ summary_of_facts,           
           + │ NVIDIA NIM     │                                          
       444 +│    Analyst     │ section     │ issues_framed[]             
           + │ Llama 3.3 70B  │                                          
       445 +├────────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────────────
           +─┼────────────────┤                                          
       446 +│ 3. Precedent   │ Body        │ ratio_decidendi, area_of_law
           + │ NVIDIA NIM     │                                          
       447 +│    Scholar     │ section     │ primary_statute,            
           + │ Llama 3.3 70B  │                                          
       448 +│                │             │ citations[] with context,   
           + │                │                                          
       449 +│                │             │ entities[]                  
           + │                │                                          
       450 +├────────────────┼─────────────┼─────────────────────────────
           +─┼────────────────┤                                          
       451 +│ 4. Compliance  │ Operative   │ disposition, winning_party, 
           + │ NVIDIA NIM     │                                          
       452 +│    Officer     │ order       │ operative_order_summary,    
           + │ Llama 3.3 70B  │                                          
       453 +│                │ section     │ court_directions[] (each    
           + │ (most critical │                                          
       454 +│                │             │   with text, responsible_   
           + │  agent)        │                                          
       455 +│                │             │   entity, action_required,  
           + │                │                                          
       456 +│                │             │   financial_details),       
           + │                │                                          
       457 +│                │             │ contempt_risk, financial[]  
           + │                │                                          
       458 +└────────────────┴─────────────┴─────────────────────────────
           +─┴────────────────┘                                          
       459 +```                                                          
       460 +                                                             
       461 +**Why 4 agents instead of one big call?**                    
       462 +- **Focused schemas** → fewer JSON parse failures and missed 
           +fields                                                       
       463 +- **Section-scoped input** → smaller per-call token budget; f
           +aster + cheaper                                              
       464 +- **Independent retry** → if Agent 3's citations fail, Agents
           + 1, 2, 4 still succeed                                       
       465 +- **Cost shaping** → only the simple metadata agent uses the 
           +cheap 8B model; the three reasoning-heavy agents use the stro
           +ng 70B model                                                 
       466 +                                                             
       467 +**Large-PDF routing:** PDFs with ≥25 pages route **all 4 agen
           +ts** through OpenRouter Llama 3.3 70B (which has larger conte
           +xt windows and no NIM rate limits). Threshold is configurable
           + via `OPENROUTER_LARGE_PDF_THRESHOLD` env var.               
       468 +                                                             
       469 +### B. Department Classifier (single-shot)                   
       470 +                                                             
       471 +```                                                          
       472 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┐                                              
       473 +│ INPUT  : operative_text + body_text + entities + parties (c
           +oncat ≤6K ch) │                                              
       474 +│ MODEL  : NVIDIA NIM Llama 3.3 70B                          
           +              │                                              
       475 +│ PROMPT : full 48-dept catalogue + Karnataka routing rules  
           +              │                                              
       476 +│ OUTPUT : { primary_code, secondary_codes[], rationale }    
           +              │                                              
       477 +│ FALLBK : keyword-scoring pass (deterministic) if LLM unreac
           +hable         │                                              
       478 +└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┘                                              
       479 +```                                                          
       480 +                                                             
       481 +The prompt encodes domain knowledge like "GST → FINANCE (Comm
           +ercial Taxes sits under Finance in Karnataka)" and "KPTCL ser
           +vice matters → ENERGY". Built-in negative examples prevent th
           +e model defaulting to HOME or TECH_EDU for ambiguous cases.  
       482 +                                                             
       483 +### C. Directive Enricher (the government-perspective lens)  
       484 +                                                             
       485 +Agent 4 extracts directives **verbatim** — that's the source-
           +of-truth record. But a department officer needs an additional
           + translation: *"is this for ME?"* and *"if so, what do I actu
           +ally do?"*                                                   
       486 +                                                             
       487 +```                                                          
       488 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┐                                              
       489 +│ INPUT  : case metadata + all extracted directives          
           +              │                                              
       490 +│ MODEL  : OpenRouter google/gemini-2.5-pro                  
           +              │                                              
       491 +│          (Gemini chosen for stronger instruction-following 
           +— Llama 70B   │                                              
       492 +│           confidently fabricates form numbers when pushed) 
           +              │                                              
       493 +│ FALLBK : NVIDIA NIM Llama 3.3 70B                          
           +              │                                              
       494 +│                                                            
           +              │                                              
       495 +│ OUTPUT (per directive):                                    
           +              │                                              
       496 +│  • actor_type ∈ { government_department, court_or_registry,
           +              │                                              
       497 +│                   accused_or_petitioner, third_party, infor
           +mational }    │                                              
       498 +│  • gov_action_required: bool                               
           +              │                                              
       499 +│  • govt_summary: 1-line plain-English restatement          
           +              │                                              
       500 +│  • implementation_steps[]: 2-4 LCO-actionable bullets (gov 
           +only)         │                                              
       501 +│  • display_note: "no action required because X" (non-gov on
           +ly)           │                                              
       502 +└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┘                                              
       503 +```                                                          
       504 +                                                             
       505 +**Anti-hallucination guardrails baked into the prompt:**     
       506 +                                                             
       507 +1. NEVER invent procedural specifics (form numbers, treasury 
           +codes, internal file IDs, deadlines) that aren't named in the
           + operative order                                             
       508 +2. Distinguish what the court ordered:                       
       509 +   - **Quashed an admin order** → reverse that administrative
           + state (e.g. unblock GST ledger) — NOT a refund              
       510 +   - **Declared a status** (exempt, eligible) → update assess
           +ment records — NOT a refund                                  
       511 +   - **Directed payment** → only THEN process a payment      
       512 +   - **Remanded** → reconsider afresh, NOT auto-grant relief 
       513 +   - **Modified award with explicit math** → recalculate per 
           +the formula AND disburse                                     
       514 +3. When in doubt, stay general ("update assessment records") 
           +rather than fabricate ("Form TCR-3")                         
       515 +                                                             
       516 +### D. RAG Recommendation Pipeline (single-agent or 4-agent) 
       517 +                                                             
       518 +For the APPEAL-vs-COMPLY recommendation:                     
       519 +                                                             
       520 +```                                                          
       521 +Case context                                                 
       522 +   │                                                         
       523 +   ▼                                                         
       524 +[Hybrid RAG]  →  Top-K legally-similar precedents (BM25 + InL
           +egalBERT + RRF + Cross-Encoder)                              
       525 +   │                                                         
       526 +   ▼                                                         
       527 +[Rules Engine]  →  Statutory appeal deadline (Limitation Act 
           ++ holidays)                                                  
       528 +   │                                                         
       529 +   ▼                                                         
       530 +[Recommendation Agents]                                      
       531 +   ├─── Single-agent mode (default — cheap, fast)            
       532 +   │     One reasoning pass over all context → APPEAL/COMPLY 
           ++ confidence + rationale                                     
       533 +   │                                                         
       534 +   └─── 4-agent mode (deeper, costlier)                      
       535 +         Agent 1 — Precedent Researcher → win-rate trend anal
           +ysis                                                         
       536 +         Agent 2 — Devil's Advocate     → pro/con arguments  
       537 +         Agent 3 — Risk Auditor         → contempt + financia
           +l risk                                                       
       538 +         Agent 4 — Decision Synthesizer → final verdict      
       539 +         (final synthesis can use Gemini 2.5 Pro for stronges
           +t reasoning)                                                 
       540 +   │                                                         
       541 +   ▼                                                         
       542 +ActionPlan.full_rag_recommendation JSON (cached — revisits sk
           +ip re-computation)

       549 +A verifier cannot trust an AI extraction without seeing the s
           +ource. NyayaDrishti highlights **the full paragraph block** t
           +he directive came from:

       552 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┐                                              
       553 +│ ALGORITHM (apps/cases/views.py :: _annotate_source_location
           +s)            │                                              
       554 +├────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┤                                              
       555 +│ 1. Build ranked snippet list from the directive text:      
           +              │                                              
       556 +│      • Longest start-of-text first (140, 100, 70, 45, 28 ch
           +ars)          │                                              
       557 +│      • Mid-text samples at offsets 50, 100, 180            
           +              │                                              
       558 +│      • Tail snippet (last 80 chars)                        
           +              │                                              
       559 +│                                                            
           +              │                                              
       560 +│ 2. For each snippet (in rank order):                       
           +              │                                              
       561 +│      For each PDF page (LAST page first — operative orders 
           +are at end):  │                                              
       562 +│         try page.search_for(snippet)                       
           +              │                                              
       563 +│         on first match → use this as the anchor            
           +              │                                              
       564 +│                                                            
           +              │                                              
       565 +│ 3. Resolve anchor rect to its containing TEXT BLOCK via    
           +              │                                              
       566 +│    page.get_text("dict") — gives line-level bboxes         
           +              │                                              
       567 +│                                                            
           +              │                                              
       568 +│ 4. Return line rects for the ENTIRE block (the full paragra
           +ph).          │                                              
       569 +│    If the directive overflows the block, walk forward to th
           +e next        │                                              
       570 +│    adjacent block (gap < 60pt) until coverage > 55%.       
           +              │                                              
       571 +└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┘                                              
       572  ```
       573  
       574 +**Why snippet-outer instead of page-outer?** If a directive's
           + paragraph spans two pages, page-outer + reverse order causes
           + the *tail* snippet on page N+1 to win before the *start* sni
           +ppet on page N gets a chance — anchoring on the wrong page. S
           +nippet-outer (earliest text first) fixes this.               
       575 +                                                             
       576 +**Frontend rendering** (`HighlightOverlay` in `VerifyActions.
           +tsx`) takes the line rects, computes min/max bbox, clamps to 
           +standard text margins, and renders a yellow paragraph band wi
           +th a side-bracket indicator. The "Show in PDF" button on each
           + card explicitly scrolls the PDF viewer to that page.        
       577 +                                                             
       578  ---
       579  
       253 -## Getting Started                                           
       580 +## Hybrid RAG Engine                                         
       581  
       582 +Built for legal-domain semantic search over 20 years of Supre
           +me Court judgments:                                          
       583 +                                                             
       584 +```                                                          
       585 +┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
           +──────────────┐                                              
       586 +│ STAGE                  │ TECHNOLOGY              │ PURPOSE 
           +               │                                             
       587 +├────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────┼─────────
           +───────────────┤                                             
       588 +│ 1. Sparse retrieval    │ BM25Okapi (rank-bm25)   │ Catch ex
           +act statute,   │                                             
       589 +│                        │                         │ citation
           +, party names  │                                             
       590 +├────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────┼─────────
           +───────────────┤                                             
       591 +│ 2. Dense retrieval     │ InLegalBERT (768-d)     │ Semantic
           + match on      │                                             
       592 +│                        │ via ChromaDB            │ legal re
           +asoning        │                                             
       593 +├────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────┼─────────
           +───────────────┤                                             
       594 +│ 3. Fusion              │ Reciprocal Rank Fusion  │ Combine 
           +sparse+dense   │                                             
       595 +│                        │ (RRF, k=60)             │ without 
           +score scaling  │                                             
       596 +├────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────┼─────────
           +───────────────┤                                             
       597 +│ 4. Rerank              │ Open-source             │ Final pr
           +ecision rank   │                                             
       598 +│                        │ cross-encoder           │         
           +               │                                             
       599 +├────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────┼─────────
           +───────────────┤                                             
       600 +│ 5. Analytics           │ DuckDB over Parquet     │ Win-rate
           + stats across  │                                             
       601 +│                        │                         │ ~431K ca
           +se chunks      │                                             
       602 +└────────────────────────┴─────────────────────────┴─────────
           +───────────────┘                                             
       603 +```                                                          
       604 +                                                             
       605 +Files: `apps/action_plans/services/rag_engine.py`, `apps/rag/
           +embedder.py`, `apps/rag/parquet_store.py`.                   
       606 +                                                             
       607 +---                                                          
       608 +                                                             
       609 +## Data Privacy & On-Premise Deployment                      
       610 +                                                             
       611 +NyayaDrishti is designed for the strict data-residency requir
           +ements of Indian digital public infrastructure:              
       612 +                                                             
       613 +| Component | Privacy posture |                              
       614 +|---|---|                                                    
       615 +| Django backend + PostgreSQL | Government datacenter |      
       616 +| React frontend (static build) | Government datacenter or CD
           +N |                                                          
       617 +| InLegalBERT (`law-ai/InLegalBERT`) | Runs **fully local** (
           +CPU or GPU) |                                                
       618 +| ChromaDB vector store | Local persistent volume |          
       619 +| DuckDB analytics | Local files only |                      
       620 +| Cross-encoder reranker | Runs local |                      
       621 +| PDF storage | Local `media/judgments/` (or S3/MinIO) |     
       622 +| LLM calls (current cloud setup) | OpenRouter + NVIDIA NIM —
           + swappable |                                                 
       623 +| LLM (air-gapped option) | Self-host via `vLLM`, `Ollama`, o
           +r NVIDIA NIM private deployment — same OpenAI-compatible inte
           +rface |                                                      
       624 +                                                             
       625 +**Zero commercial-cloud lock-in.** Every external API uses th
           +e OpenAI-compatible chat-completions interface, so any cloud 
           +LLM provider can be swapped for a locally-hosted Llama / Mist
           +ral / Qwen / Gemma model with one environment-variable change
           +.                                                            
       626 +                                                             
       627 +---                                                          
       628 +                                                             
       629 +## Tech Stack                                                
       630 +                                                             
       631 +| Layer | Technology | Purpose |                             
       632 +|---|---|---|                                                
       633 +| **Frontend SPA** | React 19, TypeScript, Vite 6 | Hot-reloa
           +d dev, optimized production build |                          
       634 +| **Styling** | Tailwind 4 (Material 3 tokens), Framer Motion
           + | Glassmorphism dark theme, smooth transitions |            
       635 +| **PDF Viewer** | react-pdf + pdfjs-dist | In-browser render
           +ing with paragraph highlights |                              
       636 +| **State** | React Context + hooks | Auth, theme, view routi
           +ng |                                                         
       637 +| **Backend** | Django 5, Django REST Framework | REST API + 
           +ORM + migrations |                                           
       638 +| **Auth** | SimpleJWT | JWT with custom claims (role + dept_
           +id + dept_code) |                                            
       639 +| **Database** | PostgreSQL (prod) / SQLite (dev) | Relationa
           +l data |                                                     
       640 +| **PDF Parsing** | PyMuPDF4LLM + PyMuPDF | Layout-aware Mark
           +down + spatial highlights |                                  
       641 +| **LLM cascade (extraction)** | OpenRouter Llama 8B + NVIDIA
           + NIM Llama 70B | Cost-shaped per-agent routing |             
       642 +| **LLM (enrichment)** | OpenRouter Gemini 2.5 Pro | Strong i
           +nstruction-following for anti-hallucination |                
       643 +| **LLM (recommendation)** | NVIDIA NIM Llama 70B (default) /
           + Gemini 2.5 Pro (4-agent final synth) | RAG-grounded reasonin
           +g |                                                          
       644 +| **Large PDF fallback** | OpenRouter Llama 3.3 70B | Pages ≥
           +25 route all 4 extractors here |                             
       645 +| **Legal embeddings** | InLegalBERT (`law-ai/InLegalBERT`) |
           + 768-d, trained on 5.4M Indian legal docs |                  
       646 +| **Vector store** | ChromaDB (persistent, local) | Dense sim
           +ilarity search |                                             
       647 +| **Sparse retrieval** | BM25Okapi (`rank-bm25`) | Keyword/ci
           +tation match |                                               
       648 +| **Reranking** | Open-source cross-encoder | Final precision
           + pass |                                                      
       649 +| **Fusion** | Reciprocal Rank Fusion | Sparse-dense score co
           +mbination |                                                  
       650 +| **Analytics** | DuckDB over Parquet | SQL over ~431K judgme
           +nt chunks |                                                  
       651 +| **Contempt risk** | Deterministic keyword classifier | No L
           +LM guesswork on legal definitions |
