       797  
       340 -### 4. (Optional) Rebuild RAG Corpus from Scratch            
       798 +### Method 1 — Bulk ingest via CLI (recommended)             
       799  
       342 -If you want to re-generate the embeddings rather than downloa
           -ding the pre-built files:                                    
       800 +```bash                                                      
       801 +cd backend                                                   
       802 +.venv\Scripts\activate                                       
       803  
       804 +# Walk every PDF in testcases/ sequentially with 8s sleep bet
           +ween                                                         
       805 +# (keeps you under NVIDIA NIM rate limits). SHA-256 hash dedu
           +p avoids                                                     
       806 +# re-extraction of files already in the DB.                  
       807 +python manage.py bulk_ingest --dir testcases/                
       808 +                                                             
       809 +# Options:                                                   
       810 +#   --sleep 4          # shorter delay if your NIM quota is h
           +ealthy                                                       
       811 +#   --skip-dedup       # force re-extraction even if a hash a
           +lready exists                                                
       812 +```                                                          
       813 +                                                             
       814 +Each PDF passes through:                                     
       815 +1. PyMuPDF4LLM Markdown conversion                           
       816 +2. Section segmentation                                      
       817 +3. 4-agent extraction                                        
       818 +4. Department classification                                 
       819 +5. Directive enrichment (Gemini 2.5 Pro)                     
       820 +6. PyMuPDF source-paragraph annotation                       
       821 +                                                             
       822 +Expected time per PDF: 30–90 seconds depending on length.    
       823 +                                                             
       824 +### Method 2 — UI upload (single file)

           +Case Analysis" file picker in the sidebar → select a PDF. The
           + upload runs the full pipeline and lands you on the case deta
           +il page when done. SHA-256 dedup returns the existing case if
           + the same file was uploaded before.

       363 -| Technique | How We Achieve It |                            
       364 -|-----------|-------------------|                            
       365 -| **Layout-aware PDF parsing** | `PyMuPDF4LLM` converts PDFs 
           -to clean Markdown preserving structure, tables, and formattin
           -g — far superior to raw text extraction |                    
       366 -| **Bi-directional regex segmenter** | Intelligently splits j
           -udgments into Header/Body/Operative sections using 37+ legal 
           -trigger patterns specific to Indian HC judgments |           
       367 -| **4 specialized LLM agents** | Each agent receives only its
           - relevant section with a strict Pydantic schema, reducing hal
           -lucination and improving field-level accuracy |              
       368 -| **Open-source LLM strategy** | Fast models for structured m
           -etadata extraction; larger models for complex legal reasoning
           - — fully swappable with self-hosted alternatives |           
       369 -| **Source location annotation** | PyMuPDF spatial search map
           -s each extracted directive back to its exact page/coordinates
           - in the PDF for verification |                               
       370 -| **Confidence scoring** | Each extraction carries an `extrac
           -tion_confidence` score; the classifier reports confidence lev
           -els for risk assessment |                                    
       371 -| **Fallback chains** | Every LLM call has retry logic with a
           -utomatic fallback ensuring extraction never fails silently |

       876  
       375 -| Technique | How We Achieve It |                            
       376 -|-----------|-------------------|                            
       377 -| **Hybrid RAG retrieval** | BM25 (sparse) + **InLegalBERT** 
           -(dense) + Reciprocal Rank Fusion + Cross-Encoder reranking — 
           -4-stage retrieval for maximum relevance |                    
       378 -| **431K+ chunk corpus** | Pre-embedded Supreme Court judgmen
           -ts (20 years) provide statistical grounding for precedent mat
           -ching |                                                      
       379 -| **DuckDB analytics** | Instant SQL queries over parquet fil
           -es compute real win-rate statistics (allowed/dismissed/partly
           - allowed rates) |                                            
       380 -| **Dual pipeline modes** | Single-agent (default, low comput
           -e) and 4-agent adversarial mode (for government on-premise se
           -rvers) — both produce APPEAL/COMPLY with full reasoning |    
       381 -| **Deterministic rules engine** | Limitation Act §4, §12 dea
           -dline computation with court calendar holiday awareness — no 
           -LLM guesswork for legal deadlines |                          
       382 -| **Court hierarchy logic** | Automatic detection of correct 
           -appellate forum (Single Judge → Division Bench → Supreme Cour
           -t) based on case type and bench composition |                
       383 -| **Contempt risk classification** | Deterministic keyword cl
           -assifier — 22 High-risk phrases + 14 Medium-risk phrases matc
           -hed against the operative order text |                       
       384 -| **Result caching** | Full recommendation JSON cached in `fu
           -ll_rag_recommendation` field — no redundant LLM calls on revi
           -sit |

           -ncing |

           - page and bounding box in the PDF via PyMuPDF spatial annotat
           -ions |

           -mpt risk levels are prominently displayed for reviewer attent
           -ion |

           -individually verified; only approved records proceed to the d
           -ashboard |

           -1/L2 review levels with full audit trail (reviewer, timestamp
           -, notes) |

           -eld on ActionPlan ensures only human-approved data reaches de
           -cision-makers |

       430 -## ML Models Used                                            
      1028 +## Management Commands                                       
      1029  
       432 -| Model | Source | Purpose | Runs On |                       
       433 -|-------|--------|---------|---------|                       
       434 -| **Open-source LLM (fast)** | Cloud API or self-hosted | Str
           -uctured extraction (Agents 1 & 4) | Cloud API / Local |      
       435 -| **Open-source LLM (large)** | Cloud API or self-hosted | Co
           -mplex legal reasoning (Agents 2 & 3) | Cloud API / Local |   
       436 -| **InLegalBERT** | `law-ai/InLegalBERT` (HuggingFace) | Lega
           -l embeddings (768-dim), trained on 5.4M Indian legal docs | L
           -ocal (CPU/GPU) |                                             
       437 -| **Keyword Classifier** | Custom rule-based | Contempt risk 
           -classification (22 high-risk + 14 medium-risk legal phrases) 
           -| Local (no GPU needed) |                                    
       438 -| **Cross-Encoder (open-source)** | HuggingFace | Cross-encod
           -er reranking for RAG | Local (CPU) |                         
       439 -| **BM25Okapi** | `rank-bm25` | Sparse keyword retrieval | Lo
           -cal (CPU) |                                                  
      1030 +```bash                                                      
      1031 +# Department + user seeding                                  
      1032 +python manage.py seed_demo_data                  # 48 depts +
           + 13 demo users (idempotent)                                  
      1033

       449 -## License                                                   
      1075 +## Evaluation Criteria Mapping                               
      1076  
       451 -This project is licensed under the MIT License.              
      1077 +### 1. Accuracy of Extraction                                
      1078 +                                                             
      1079 +| Technique | How NyayaDrishti achieves it |                 
      1080 +|---|---|                                                    
      1081 +| **Layout-aware PDF parsing** | `PyMuPDF4LLM` produces clean
           + Markdown preserving structure, tables, and reading order — f
           +ar superior to raw text extraction |                         
      1082 +| **Bi-directional regex segmenter** | 37+ legal trigger patt
           +erns specific to Indian HC judgments; bidirectional scan ensu
           +res no reasoning is lost at boundaries |                     
      1083 +| **4 specialized LLM agents** | Each agent gets only its sec
           +tion + a strict Pydantic schema. Single-responsibility prompt
           +s reduce hallucination |                                     
      1084 +| **Cost-shaped LLM cascade** | Cheap 8B model for simple hea
           +der parsing; strong 70B for reasoning-heavy facts/issues/oper
           +ative agents |                                               
      1085 +| **Source highlighting** | PyMuPDF block-level resolution ma
           +ps each directive to its **full paragraph** in the PDF for vi
           +sual verification |                                          
      1086 +| **Fallback chains** | Every LLM call has retry + provider f
           +allback. NVIDIA NIM → OpenRouter; OpenRouter → NVIDIA NIM as 
           +needed |                                                     
      1087 +| **Per-case anti-hallucination enrichment** | Gemini 2.5 Pro
           + with explicit prompt guardrails against fabricating form num
           +bers / codes / deadlines |                                   
      1088 +| **SHA-256 dedup** | Same PDF uploaded twice short-circuits 
           +to the existing case — no spurious re-extraction |           
      1089 +                                                             
      1090 +### 2. Quality of Action Plan Generation                     
      1091 +                                                             
      1092 +| Technique | How NyayaDrishti achieves it |                 
      1093 +|---|---|                                                    
      1094 +| **Hybrid RAG retrieval** | BM25 + InLegalBERT + RRF + cross
           +-encoder rerank — 4-stage retrieval for max relevance |      
      1095 +| **431K-chunk corpus** | Pre-embedded SC judgments (20 years
           +) provide statistical grounding |                            
      1096 +| **DuckDB analytics** | Real win-rate statistics over parque
           +t (allowed/dismissed/partly allowed rates) |                 
      1097 +| **Government-perspective enricher** | Per-directive impleme
           +ntation steps + actor classification — directly answers "what
           + does my dept do?" |                                         
      1098 +| **Karnataka-specific routing rules** | Dept classifier prom
           +pt encodes state-specific knowledge (GST→FINANCE, KPTCL→ENERG
           +Y, etc.) |                                                   
      1099 +| **Single- + 4-agent recommendation** | Cheap default mode +
           + adversarial mode for on-premise servers |                   
      1100 +| **Deterministic rules engine** | Limitation Act §4/§12 + co
           +urt holiday calendar → never trust the LLM for date math |   
      1101 +| **Court hierarchy logic** | Automatic appellate forum detec
           +tion (Single Judge → Division Bench → SC) |                  
      1102 +| **Result caching** | `full_rag_recommendation` JSON cache —
           + revisits skip LLM re-run |                                  
      1103 +                                                             
      1104 +### 3. Effectiveness of Human Verification                   
      1105 +                                                             
      1106 +| Feature | How NyayaDrishti achieves it |                   
      1107 +|---|---|                                                    
      1108 +| **Side-by-side PDF viewer** | `react-pdf` renders original 
           +judgment alongside extracted data |                          
      1109 +| **Full-paragraph source highlighting** | PyMuPDF block reso
           +lution — every line of the directive's paragraph is highlight
           +ed, not just one phrase |                                    
      1110 +| **Explicit Show-in-PDF button** | Card click highlights wit
           +hout scrolling; explicit button triggers the jump |          
      1111 +| **Auto-collapse sidebar in Verify tab** | Maximises horizon
           +tal space for the PDF viewer |                               
      1112 +| **Editable AI action plans** | HLC can rewrite the AI's gov
           +t summary + implementation steps inline |                    
      1113 +| **Government Perspective Panel** | Green-bordered card per 
           +directive shows actor type + steps; muted card for non-gov in
           +formational items |                                          
      1114 +| **Per-directive verified flag** | HLC ticks each directive 
           +individually; only ticked items reach LCO Execution |        
      1115 +| **Server-side role enforcement** | Backend 403s non-HLC wri
           +tes — UI gating is cosmetic, not the security boundary |     
      1116 +| **Multi-level review chain** | `ReviewLog` with L1/L2 revie
           +w levels, audit trail (reviewer, timestamp, notes, action) | 
      1117 +                                                             
      1118 +### 4. Clarity and Usability of Dashboard                    
      1119 +                                                             
      1120 +| Feature | How NyayaDrishti achieves it |                   
      1121 +|---|---|                                                    
      1122 +| **Material 3 glassmorphism** | Dark theme with `glass-card`
           + surfaces, blue accents, smooth Framer Motion transitions |  
      1123 +| **Role-based default landing** | LCO → Execution, Nodal → D
           +eadlines, Central Law → 48-tile grid, HLC → Dashboard |      
      1124 +| **Live database-driven stats** | Real-time totals, pending 
           +review, high-risk count, upcoming deadlines |                
      1125 +| **30-day deadline heatmap** | Visual calendar from actual c
           +ompliance/appeal dates |                                     
      1126 +| **Risk board** | Priority-sorted by contempt risk + days re
           +maining |                                                    
      1127 +| **Department drill-down** | Click any of the 48 tiles → fil
           +tered case list with breadcrumb chip |                       
      1128 +| **Government-of-Karnataka branding** | State crest in sideb
           +ar, official tagline |                                       
      1129 +| **Responsive layouts** | Phone / tablet / desktop breakpoin
           +ts throughout |
